***завоз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́з</a> (31562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavóz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>the act of delivering, usually of something heavy, unwieldy, or in large quantities
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завоз.html>заво́з</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происходить.html>происхо́дит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavóz</b> továra v magazín proisxódit nóčʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the store is being restocked (goods being delivered) at night</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завозить.html>завози́ть</a> (21403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завозить.html>завози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завезти.html>завезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to a place</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to drop off <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at a place</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to supply, to deliver</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завозить.html>завози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to carry <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to begin to transport</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dirty, to contaminate</li></ol>

***заволакивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заволакивать.html>завола́кивать</a> (28878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заволо́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavolók-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заволакивать.html>завола́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavolákivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заволочь.html>заволо́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obscure, to cloud (the sun, the sky, one's eyes with tears, etc.)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворожить.html>заворожи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavorožítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***заворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a> (11818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">завороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">завороти́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to screw tight, to tighten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кран.html>кран</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> kran</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn off the tap</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck up, to roll up</li>
<li>to wrap up <i>(in)</i></li>
<li>to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> za úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn (round) the corner</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивай</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivaj</b> otsjúda!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turn back!; go away from here!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in <i>(at a place)</i>, to call <i>(at a place)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mojó zajavlénije zavernúli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my application was turned down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукопись.html>ру́копись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:издательство.html>изда́тельстве</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó rúkopisʹ zavernúli v izdátelʹstve</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he got a rejection slip from the publisher</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin, to come on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́зы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zavernúli morózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frosts came on</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, to utter, to let loose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nu, ty i zavernúl rečʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">some speech you made!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, to manage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> bolʹšimi delámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run a big business, be a big boss</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заворо́чать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavoróčatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворочаться.html>заворо́чаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavoróčatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворочаться.html>воро́чаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start to toss and turn <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the whole body</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to turn, to start to roll <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of something heavy or bulky</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заворо́чать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavoróčatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заворчать.html>заворча́ть</a> (17697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворчать.html>ворча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorčátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворчать.html>заворча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavorčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворчать.html>ворча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to grumble</li>
<li>to begin to growl</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завхоз.html>завхо́з</a> (13566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведующий.html>заве́дующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йством</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavédujuščij xozjájstvom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завхоз.html>завхо́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavxóz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завхоз.html>завхо́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завхоз.html>завхо́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завхоз.html>завхо́зов</a></b>)
</p>
